    <h2>
     <a id="_ELBO__0">
     </a>
     变分扩散模型 ELBO 重构推导详解
    </h2>
    <p>
     在变分扩散模型（Variational Diffusion Model）中，证据下界（Evidence Lower Bound, ELBO）的形式通过优化正向和逆向分布的匹配来实现数据生成。初始 ELBO （
     <a href="https://lishizheng.blog.csdn.net/article/details/146041186?spm=1001.2014.3001.5502" rel="nofollow">
      变分扩散模型中的 Evidence Lower Bound (ELBO) 详解
     </a>
     ）存在采样复杂性，尤其是过渡块中需要联合分布 (
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        q 
         
        
          φ 
         
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           + 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         ∣ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        q_φ(x_{t-1}, x_{t+1}|x_0)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0361em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           q
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 φ
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>

            <span class="vlist-r">

         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x

                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  t
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>

             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​

            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
              <span class="">

            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  t
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin mtight">
                  +
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          ∣
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 0
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ) 的样本，这引发了重新设计的动机。后面提出了一种等价的 ELBO 形式，通过贝叶斯定理和条件调整简化了计算。本文将详细推导这一重构过程，解释这种转变，面向具备概率论和深度学习基础的读者。
    </p>
    <p>
     参考：https://arxiv.org/pdf/2403.18103
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ELBO__8">
     </a>
     初始 ELBO 的问题
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="_ELBO_10">
     </a>
     原始 ELBO
    </h4>
    <p>
     原本定义的 ELBO 为：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         ELBO 
          
          
          
            φ 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            θ

          x

             q

          [ 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
         
           p 
          
         
           θ 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          ∣ 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
          )

          − 
         
         
         
           E

            x

             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ∥ 
          
         
           p 
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            T 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
          − 
         
         
         
           ∑ 
          
          
          
            t 
           
          
            = 
           
          
            1 
           
          
          
          
            T 
           
          
            − 
           
          
            1 
           
          
         
         
         
           E 
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x

           [ 
          
          
          
            D 
           
           
           
             K 
            
           
             L 
            
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            q 
           
          
            φ 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            t 
           
          
         
           ∣ 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             t 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ∥ 
          
          
          
            p 
           
          
            θ 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            t 
           
          
         
           ∣ 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             t 
            
           
             + 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
       
         \text{ELBO}_{φ,θ}(x) = \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_1|x_0)} [\log p_θ(x_0|x_1)] - \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_{T-1}|x_0)} \left[ D_{KL}(q_φ(x_T|x_{T-1}) \| p(x_T)) \right] - \sum_{t=1}^{T-1} \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_{t-1}, x_{t+1}|x_0)} \left[ D_{KL}(q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}) \| p_θ(x_t|x_{t+1})) \right]
        </span>

             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                </span>
                <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                   t
                  </span>
                  <span class="mbin mtight">
                   +
                  </span>
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   1
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-s">
               ​
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
               <span class="">
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
      ) 的样本。
     </li>
     <li>
      目标是简化一致性检查，避免“反向”依赖。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="_32">
     </a>
     贝叶斯定理的引入
    </h4>
    <p>
     通过贝叶斯定理调整条件分布：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">

    <h3>
     <a id="_ELBO__50">
     </a>
     重构 ELBO 的推导
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="_1_Jensen__52">
     </a>
     步骤 1：从 Jensen 不等式开始
    </h4>
    <p>
     从之前的基础推导（
     <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/shizheng_Li/article/details/146044283?sharetype=blogdetail&amp;sharerId=146044283&amp;sharerefer=PC&amp;sharesource=shizheng_Li&amp;spm=1011.2480.3001.8118">
      变分扩散模型 ELBO 的推导过程详解
     </a>
     ）出发：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
        
          p 
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ≥ 
         
         
         
           E 
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              1 
             
            
              : 
             
            
              T 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
         
         
           [ 
          
         
           log 
          
         
           ⁡ 
          
          
           
           
             p 
            
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              x 
             
             
             
               0 
              
             
               :

              x 
             
            
              0 
             
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
       
         \log p(x) \geq \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_{1:T}|x_0)} \left[ \log \frac{p(x_{0:T})}{q_φ(x_{1:T}|x_0)} \right]
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mop">

          </span>

          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord mathbb">
            E
           </span>
           <span class="msupsub">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                </span>
                <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">

                    q
                   </span>
                   <span class="msupsub">
                    <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                     <span class="vlist-r">
                      <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1645em;">
                       <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                        <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                        </span>
                        <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                         <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                          φ

                    <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                     <span class="vlist-r">
                      <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;">
                       <span class="" style="top: -2.3567em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                        <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                        </span>
                        <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                         <span class="mord mtight">
                          <span class="mord mtight">
                           1

                      </span>
                      <span class="vlist-s">
                       ​

                  </span>
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   ∣
                  </span>
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                   <span class="msupsub">
                    <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">

    <h4>
     <a id="_2_71">
     </a>
     步骤 2：展开对数项
    </h4>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
          
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              0 
             
            
              : 
             
            
              T 
             
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              1 
             
            
              : 
             
            
              T 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
          
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             T 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
           
           
             ∏ 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              = 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             T 
            
           
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
           
           
             ∏ 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              = 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             T 
            
           
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            , 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
       
         \log \frac{p(x_{0:T})}{q_φ(x_{1:T}|x_0)} = \log \frac{p(x_T) p(x_0|x_1) \prod_{t=2}^T p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_1|x_0) \prod_{t=2}^T q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}, x_0)}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 2.3991em; vertical-align: -0.9721em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mop">
           lo
           <span style="margin-right: 0.0139em;">
            g
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
           </span>
           <span class="mfrac">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.314em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord">
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                   q
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                         φ

                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">

                  </span>

                 <span class="mopen">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal">
                   x
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mtight">
                         <span class="mord mtight">
                          1
                         </span>
                         <span class="mrel mtight">
                          :
                         </span>
                         <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
                          T
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                      <span class="">
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  ∣
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal">
                   x
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">

    <p>
     分离：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         = 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
          
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             T 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
          + 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
          
           
           
             ∏ 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              = 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             T 
            
           
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             ∏ 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              = 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             T 
            
           
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            , 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
       
         = \log \frac{p(x_T) p(x_0|x_1)}{q_φ(x_1|x_0)} + \log \frac{\prod_{t=2}^T p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{\prod_{t=2}^T q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}, x_0)}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mrel">
           =
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 2.3991em; vertical-align: -0.9721em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mop">
           lo
           <span style="margin-right: 0.0139em;">
            g
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
           </span>
           <span class="mfrac">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">

    <h4>
     <a id="_3_82">
     </a>
     步骤 3：应用贝叶斯调整
    </h4>
    <p>
     对第二项，使用贝叶斯定理：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            , 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
         
          
          
            p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
            
            
              t 
             
            
              − 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            , 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
           
            
             
             
               q 
              
             
               φ 
              
             
            
              ( 
             
             
             
               x 
              
             
               t 
              
             
            
              ∣ 
             
             
             
               x 
              
             
               0 
              
             
            
              ) 
             
            
            
             
             
               q 
              
             
               φ 
              
             
            
              ( 
             
             
             
               x 
              
              
              
                t 
               
              
                − 
               
              
                1 
               
              
             
            
              ∣ 
             
             
             
               x 
              
             
               0 
              
             
            
              ) 
             
            
           
          
         
        
       
         \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}, x_0)} = \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0) \frac{q_φ(x_t|x_0)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_0)}}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 2.3991em; vertical-align: -0.9721em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
           </span>
           <span class="mfrac">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.427em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.314em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord">
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                   q
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                         φ
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
                      <span class="">
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="mopen">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal">
                   x
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                         t
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">

         = \frac{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0) q_φ(x_t|x_0)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_0)} \cdot \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0)}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;">

        <span class="katex-mathml">

         \prod_{t=2}^T \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}, x_0)} = \prod_{t=2}^T \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0)} \cdot \frac{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_0)}{q_φ(x_t|x_0)}
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 3.0954em; vertical-align: -1.2671em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mop op-limits">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.8283em;">

     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         = 
         
         
         
           E 
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            (

           E

            (

             ) 
            
           
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
       
         = \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_1|x_0)} [\log p_θ(x_0|x_1)] + \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_{1:T}|x_0)} \left[ \log \frac{p(x_T)}{q_φ(x_T|x_0)} \right]

     使用贝叶斯调整：

       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         p 
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x

         \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_t|x_{t-1}, x_0)} = \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t) q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_0)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0) q_φ(x_t|x_0)}

    <p>
     第二项的和为：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             T 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
          = 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
         
           q 
          
         
           φ 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
          ∣ 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          − 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
         
           q 
          
         
           φ 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           T 
          
         
        
          ∣ 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
       
         \log \frac{q_φ(x_1|x_0)}{q_φ(x_T|x_0)} = \log q_φ(x_1|x_0) - \log q_φ(x_T|x_0)
        </span>

          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     但重点是第一项：
    </p>

         \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_{t-1}, x_t|x_0)} \left[ \log \frac{p(x_{t-1}|x_t)}{q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0)} \right] = -\mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_t|x_0)} \left[ D_{KL}(q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0) \| p_θ(x_{t-1}|x_t)) \right]

    <h4>
     <a id="_ELBO_163">
     </a>
     最终 ELBO
    </h4>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--display">
      <span class="katex-display">
       <span class="katex">
        <span class="katex-mathml">
         ELBO 
          
          
          
            φ 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            θ 
           
          
         
        
          ( 
         
        
          x 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          = 
         
         
         
           E 
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
        
          [ 
         
        
          log 
         
        
          ⁡ 
         
         
         
           p 
          
         
           θ 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          ∣ 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ] 
         
        
          − 
         
         
         
           D 
          
          
          
            K 
           
          
            L 
           
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           q 
          
         
           φ 
          
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           T 
          
         
        
          ∣ 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ∥ 
         
        
          p 
         
        
          ( 
         
         
         
           x 
          
         
           T 
          
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          ) 
         
        
          − 
         
         
         
           ∑ 
          
          
          
            t 
           
          
            = 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           T 
          
         
         
         
           E 
          
          
           
           
             q 
            
           
             φ 
            
           
          
            ( 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             t 
            
           
          
            ∣ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             0 
            
           
          
            ) 
           
          
         
         
         
           [ 
          
          
          
            D 
           
           
           
             K 
            
           
             L 
            
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            q 
           
          
            φ 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             t 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           ∣ 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            t 
           
          
         
           , 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            0 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ∥ 
          
          
          
            p 
           
          
            θ 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             t 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           ∣ 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            t 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
       
         \text{ELBO}_{φ,θ}(x) = \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_1|x_0)} [\log p_θ(x_0|x_1)] - D_{KL}(q_φ(x_T|x_0) \| p(x_T)) - \sum_{t=2}^T \mathbb{E}_{q_φ(x_t|x_0)} \left[ D_{KL}(q_φ(x_{t-1}|x_t, x_0) \| p_θ(x_{t-1}|x_t)) \right]
        </span>
        <span class="katex-html">
         <span class="base">
          <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0361em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
          </span>
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord text">
            <span class="mord">
             ELBO
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="msupsub">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;">
               <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                </span>
                <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                   φ

                  <span class="mpunct mtight">

                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
                   θ

                     <span class="vlist-r">

                       <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">

                     <span class="vlist-r">

                       <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">

                    <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                     <span class="vlist-r">

                       <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">

                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            ))
           </span>
           <span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">
            ]
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>

     </li>
     <li>
      新的 ELBO 保持优化目标，简化了采样复杂性。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_177">
     </a>
     代码实现片段（伪代码）
    </h3>
    <pre><code class="prism language-python"><span class="token keyword">def</span> <span class="token function">elbo_loss_new</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> model<span class="token punctuation">,</span> T<span class="token punctuation">,</span> alpha_schedule<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
    elbo <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">0.0</span>
    x1 <span class="token operator">=</span> forward_transition<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> alpha_schedule<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    elbo <span class="token operator">+=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>log_prob_x0_given_x1<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> x1<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># Reconstruction</span>
    
    xT <span class="token operator">=</span> forward_multi_step<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> alpha_schedule<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    kl_prior <span class="token operator">=</span> kl_divergence<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xT<span class="token punctuation">,</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>zeros_like<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ones_like<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
    elbo <span class="token operator">-=</span> kl_prior  <span class="token comment"># Prior matching</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">for</span> t <span class="token keyword">in</span> <span class="token builtin">range</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> T <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span>
        xt <span class="token operator">=</span> forward_step<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> t<span class="token punctuation">,</span> alpha_schedule<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        xt_minus_1 <span class="token operator">=</span> forward_step<span class="token punctuation">(</span>x0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> t <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> alpha_schedule<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        kl_cons <span class="token operator">=</span> kl_divergence<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xt_minus_1<span class="token punctuation">,</span> model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>reverse_mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xt<span class="token punctuation">,</span> t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> model<span class="token punctuation">.</span>reverse_cov<span class="token punctuation">(</span>xt<span class="token punctuation">,</span> t<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
        elbo <span class="token operator">-=</span> torch<span class="token punctuation">.</span>mean<span class="token punctuation">(</span>kl_cons<span class="token punctuation">)</span>  <span class="token comment"># Consistency</span>
    
    <span class="token keyword">return</span> elbo
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_200">
     </a>
     总结
    </h3>
    <p>
     重构后的 ELBO 通过贝叶斯调整消除了联合采样的复杂性，保持了模型的优化能力。这一设计体现了扩散模型的灵活性，为高效训练提供了可能。
    </p>
    <p>
     希望这篇推导帮助你理解！
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_206">
     </a>
     后记
    </h3>
    <p>
     2025年3月5日18点17分于上海，在grok 3大模型辅助下完成。
    </p>
